Local Open Scope cat.

(**
The definition of a Street opfibration of categories
 *)
Section StreetOpFibration.
  Context {E B : category}
          (F : E ⟶ B).

  Definition is_opcartesian_sopfib
             {e₁ e₂ : E}
             (f : e₁--> e₂)
    : UU
    := ∏ (e₃ : E)
         (g : e₁ --> e₃)
         (h : F e₂ --> F e₃)
         (p : #F g = #F f · h),
       ∃! (φ : e₂ --> e₃),
       #F φ = h
       ×
       f · φ = g.

  
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
isaprop (is_opcartesian_sopfib f)

  
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
isaprop (is_opcartesian_sopfib f)

    
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
t: E
t0: E ⟦ e₁, t ⟧
t1: B ⟦ F e₂, F t ⟧
t2: # F t0 = # F f · t1
isofhlevel 1
  (∃! φ : E ⟦ e₂, t ⟧, # F φ = t1 × f · φ = t0)

    apply isapropiscontr.
  Qed.

  Definition opcartesian_factorization_sopfib
             {e₁ e₂ : E}
             {f : e₁--> e₂}
             (Hf : is_opcartesian_sopfib f)
             {e₃ : E}
             (g : e₁ --> e₃)
             (h : F e₂ --> F e₃)
             (p : #F g = #F f · h)
    : e₂ --> e₃
    := pr11 (Hf e₃ g h p).

  Definition opcartesian_factorization_sopfib_over
             {e₁ e₂ : E}
             {f : e₁--> e₂}
             (Hf : is_opcartesian_sopfib f)
             {e₃ : E}
             (g : e₁ --> e₃)
             (h : F e₂ --> F e₃)
             (p : #F g = #F f · h)
    : #F (opcartesian_factorization_sopfib Hf g h p) = h
    := pr121 (Hf e₃ g h p).

  Definition opcartesian_factorization_sopfib_commute
             {e₁ e₂ : E}
             {f : e₁--> e₂}
             (Hf : is_opcartesian_sopfib f)
             {e₃ : E}
             (g : e₁ --> e₃)
             (h : F e₂ --> F e₃)
             (p : #F g = #F f · h)
    : f · opcartesian_factorization_sopfib Hf g h p = g
    := pr221 (Hf e₃ g h p).

  
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
Hf: is_opcartesian_sopfib f
e₃: E
g: E ⟦ e₁, e₃ ⟧
h: B ⟦ F e₂, F e₃ ⟧
p: # F g = # F f · h
φ₁, φ₂: E ⟦ e₂, e₃ ⟧
p₁: # F φ₁ = h
p₂: # F φ₂ = h
q₁: f · φ₁ = g
q₂: f · φ₂ = g
φ₁ = φ₂

  
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
Hf: is_opcartesian_sopfib f
e₃: E
g: E ⟦ e₁, e₃ ⟧
h: B ⟦ F e₂, F e₃ ⟧
p: # F g = # F f · h
φ₁, φ₂: E ⟦ e₂, e₃ ⟧
p₁: # F φ₁ = h
p₂: # F φ₂ = h
q₁: f · φ₁ = g
q₂: f · φ₂ = g
φ₁ = φ₂

    exact (maponpaths
             pr1
             (proofirrelevance
                _
                (isapropifcontr (Hf e₃ g h p))
                (φ₁ ,, p₁ ,, q₁)
                (φ₂ ,, p₂ ,, q₂))).
  Defined.

  Definition street_opfib
    : UU
    := ∏ (e : E)
         (b : B)
         (f : F e --> b),
       ∑ (bb : E)
         (ff_i : e --> bb × z_iso b (F bb)),
       # F (pr1 ff_i) = f · pr2 ff_i
       ×
       is_opcartesian_sopfib (pr1 ff_i).
End StreetOpFibration.

(**
The projection of an opfibration is a Street opfibration
 *)
Section OpcleavingToStreetOpFib.
  Context {B : category}
          {D : disp_cat B}.

  Let E : category := total_category D.
  Let P : E ⟶ B := pr1_category D.

  
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_opcartesian (pr2 f)
z: E
g: E ⟦ e₁, z ⟧
h: B ⟦ P e₂, P z ⟧
p: # P g = # P f · h
isaprop (∑ φ : E ⟦ e₂, z ⟧, # P φ = h × f · φ = g)

  
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_opcartesian (pr2 f)
z: E
g: E ⟦ e₁, z ⟧
h: B ⟦ P e₂, P z ⟧
p: # P g = # P f · h
isaprop (∑ φ : E ⟦ e₂, z ⟧, # P φ = h × f · φ = g)

    
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_opcartesian (pr2 f)
z: E
g: E ⟦ e₁, z ⟧
h: B ⟦ P e₂, P z ⟧
p: # P g = # P f · h
lift:= H (pr1 z) (pr2 z) h
(transportf (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧, pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z) p (pr2 g)): ∃! gg : pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z,
(pr2 f ;; gg)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧,
   pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z) p 
  (pr2 g)
isaprop (∑ φ : E ⟦ e₂, z ⟧, # P φ = h × f · φ = g)

   pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z) p

isProofIrrelevant
  (∑ φ : E ⟦ e₂, z ⟧, # P φ = h × f · φ = g)

B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_opcartesian (pr2 f)
z: E
g: E ⟦ e₁, z ⟧
h: B ⟦ P e₂, P z ⟧
p: # P g = # P f · h
lift:= H (pr1 z) (pr2 z) h
(transportf (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧, pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z) p (pr2 g)): ∃! gg : pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z,
(pr2 f ;; gg)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧,
   pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z) p 
  (pr2 g)
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ φ : E ⟦ e₂, z ⟧, # P φ = h × f · φ = g
φφ₁:= transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 e₂, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₂ -->[ z0] pr2 z) 
  (pr12 φ₁) (pr21 φ₁): pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z
φφ₂:= transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 e₂, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₂ -->[ z0] pr2 z) 
  (pr12 φ₂) (pr21 φ₂): pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z
(pr2 f ;; φφ₁)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ w : B ⟦ pr1 e₁, pr1 z ⟧, pr2 e₁ -->[ w] pr2 z) p
  (pr2 g)

  (pr2 g)

  (pr12 φ₁ @ ! pr12 φ₂) (pr21 φ₁) = pr21 φ₂

P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_opcartesian (pr2 f)
z: E
g: E ⟦ e₁, z ⟧
h: B ⟦ P e₂, P z ⟧
p: # P g = # P f · h
lift:= H (pr1 z) (pr2 z) h
(transportf (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧, pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z) p (pr2 g)): ∃! gg : pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z,
(pr2 f ;; gg)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧,
   pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z) p 
  (pr2 g)
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ φ : E ⟦ e₂, z ⟧, # P φ = h × f · φ = g
φφ₁:= transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 e₂, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₂ -->[ z0] pr2 z) 
  (pr12 φ₁) (pr21 φ₁): pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z
φφ₂:= transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 e₂, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₂ -->[ z0] pr2 z) 
  (pr12 φ₂) (pr21 φ₂): pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z
H₁: (pr2 f ;; φφ₁)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ w : B ⟦ pr1 e₁, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₁ -->[ w] pr2 z) p 
  (pr2 g)
(pr2 f ;; φφ₂)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ w : B ⟦ pr1 e₁, pr1 z ⟧, pr2 e₁ -->[ w] pr2 z) p
  (pr2 g)

  (pr12 φ₁) (pr21 φ₁): pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z

  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 e₂, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₂ -->[ z0] pr2 z) 
  (pr12 φ₂) (pr21 φ₂): pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z
H₁: (pr2 f ;; φφ₁)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ w : B ⟦ pr1 e₁, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₁ -->[ w] pr2 z) p 
  (pr2 g)
H₂: (pr2 f ;; φφ₂)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ w : B ⟦ pr1 e₁, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₁ -->[ w] pr2 z) p 
  (pr2 g)
q:= proofirrelevance
  (∑ gg : pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z,
   (pr2 f ;; gg)%mor_disp =
   transportf
     (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧, pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z)
     p (pr2 g)) (isapropifcontr lift): isProofIrrelevant
  (∑ gg : pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z,
   (pr2 f ;; gg)%mor_disp =
   transportf
     (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧,
      pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z) p 
     (pr2 g))
transportf (mor_disp (pr2 e₂) (pr2 z))
  (pr12 φ₁ @ ! pr12 φ₂) (pr21 φ₁) = pr21 φ₂

     (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧, pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z)
     p (pr2 g)) (isapropifcontr lift): isProofIrrelevant
  (∑ gg : pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z,
   (pr2 f ;; gg)%mor_disp =
   transportf
     (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧,
      pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z) p 
     (pr2 g))
r: transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 e₂, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₂ -->[ z0] pr2 z) 
  (pr12 φ₁) (pr21 φ₁) =
transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 e₂, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₂ -->[ z0] pr2 z) 
  (pr12 φ₂) (pr21 φ₂)
transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 e₂, pr1 z ⟧, pr2 e₂ -->[ z0] pr2 z)
  (pr12 φ₂ @ ! pr12 φ₂) (pr21 φ₂) = pr21 φ₂
 
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_opcartesian (pr2 f)
z: E
g: E ⟦ e₁, z ⟧
h: B ⟦ P e₂, P z ⟧
p: # P g = # P f · h
lift:= H (pr1 z) (pr2 z) h
(transportf (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧, pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z) p (pr2 g)): ∃! gg : pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z,
(pr2 f ;; gg)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧,
   pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z) p 
  (pr2 g)
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ φ : E ⟦ e₂, z ⟧, # P φ = h × f · φ = g
φφ₁:= transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 e₂, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₂ -->[ z0] pr2 z) 
  (pr12 φ₁) (pr21 φ₁): pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z
φφ₂:= transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 e₂, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₂ -->[ z0] pr2 z) 
  (pr12 φ₂) (pr21 φ₂): pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z
H₁: (pr2 f ;; φφ₁)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ w : B ⟦ pr1 e₁, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₁ -->[ w] pr2 z) p 
  (pr2 g)
H₂: (pr2 f ;; φφ₂)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ w : B ⟦ pr1 e₁, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₁ -->[ w] pr2 z) p 
  (pr2 g)
q:= proofirrelevance
  (∑ gg : pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z,
   (pr2 f ;; gg)%mor_disp =
   transportf
     (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧, pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z)
     p (pr2 g)) (isapropifcontr lift): isProofIrrelevant
  (∑ gg : pr2 e₂ -->[ h] pr2 z,
   (pr2 f ;; gg)%mor_disp =
   transportf
     (λ z0 : B ⟦ P e₁, P z ⟧,
      pr2 e₁ -->[ z0] pr2 z) p 
     (pr2 g))
r: transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 e₂, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₂ -->[ z0] pr2 z) 
  (pr12 φ₁) (pr21 φ₁) =
transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 e₂, pr1 z ⟧,
   pr2 e₂ -->[ z0] pr2 z) 
  (pr12 φ₂) (pr21 φ₂)
isaset (B ⟦ P e₂, P z ⟧)

      apply homset_property.
  Qed.

φφ₁:= g,, pr1 φ₁ : E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧: E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧
pr1 f · g,, (pr2 f ;; pr1 φ₁)%mor_disp =
pr1 f · g,, gf

D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_opcartesian_sopfib P f
z: B
g: B ⟦ pr1 e₂, z ⟧
zz: D z
gf: pr2 e₁ -->[ pr1 f · g] zz
lift:= H (z,, zz) (pr1 f · g,, gf) g (idpath (# P (pr1 f · g,, gf))): ∃! φ : E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧,
# P φ = g × f · φ = pr1 f · g,, gf
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ gg : pr2 e₂ -->[ g] zz,
(pr2 f ;; gg)%mor_disp = gf
φφ₁:= g,, pr1 φ₁ : E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧: E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧
g = g
 apply idpath.

D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_opcartesian_sopfib P f
z: B
g: B ⟦ pr1 e₂, z ⟧

lift:= H (z,, zz) (pr1 f · g,, gf) g (idpath (# P (pr1 f · g,, gf))): ∃! φ : E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧,
# P φ = g × f · φ = pr1 f · g,, gf
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ gg : pr2 e₂ -->[ g] zz,
(pr2 f ;; gg)%mor_disp = gf
φφ₁:= g,, pr1 φ₁ : E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧: E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧
H₁: # P φφ₁ = g × f · φφ₁ = pr1 f · g,, gf
φφ₂:= g,, pr1 φ₂ : E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧: E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧
H₂: # P φφ₂ = g × f · φφ₂ = pr1 f · g,, gf
q: φφ₁ = φφ₂
transportf (λ x : B ⟦ pr1 e₂, z ⟧, pr2 e₂ -->[ x] zz)
  (base_paths φφ₁ φφ₂ q) (pr2 φφ₁) = pr1 φ₁

    
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_opcartesian_sopfib P f
z: B
g: B ⟦ pr1 e₂, z ⟧
zz: D z
gf: pr2 e₁ -->[ pr1 f · g] zz
lift:= H (z,, zz) (pr1 f · g,, gf) g (idpath (# P (pr1 f · g,, gf))): ∃! φ : E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧,
# P φ = g × f · φ = pr1 f · g,, gf
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ gg : pr2 e₂ -->[ g] zz,
(pr2 f ;; gg)%mor_disp = gf
φφ₁:= g,, pr1 φ₁ : E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧: E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧
H₁: # P φφ₁ = g × f · φφ₁ = pr1 f · g,, gf
φφ₂:= g,, pr1 φ₂ : E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧: E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧
H₂: # P φφ₂ = g × f · φφ₂ = pr1 f · g,, gf
q: φφ₁ = φφ₂
isaset (B ⟦ pr1 e₂, z ⟧)

    apply homset_property.
  Qed.

P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_opcartesian_sopfib P f
is_opcartesian (pr2 f)

lift:= H (z,, zz) (pr1 f · g,, gf) g (idpath (# P (pr1 f · g,, gf))): ∃! φ : E ⟦ e₂, z,, zz ⟧,
# P φ = g × f · φ = pr1 f · g,, gf
isaprop
  (∑ gg : pr2 e₂ -->[ g] zz,
   (pr2 f ;; gg)%mor_disp = gf)

b: B

# F ff₂ = # F ff₁ · (inv_from_z_iso β₁ · β₂)

  abstract
    (rewrite over₁, over₂ ;
     rewrite !assoc' ;
     apply maponpaths ;
     rewrite !assoc ;
     rewrite z_iso_inv_after_z_iso ;
     rewrite id_left ;
     apply idpath).
Defined.

Section UniqueLifts.
  Context {E B : category}
          (F : E ⟶ B)
          {e : E}
          {b : B}
          (f : F e --> b)
          (bb₁ bb₂ : E)
          (ff₁ : e --> bb₁)
          (β₁ : z_iso b (F bb₁))
          (ff₂ :  e --> bb₂)
          (β₂ : z_iso b (F bb₂))
          (over₁ : # F (ff₁) = f · β₁)
          (over₂ : # F (ff₂) = f · β₂)
          (cart₁ : is_opcartesian_sopfib F ff₁)
          (cart₂ : is_opcartesian_sopfib F ff₂).

  Let ζ : bb₁ --> bb₂
    := lift_unique_sopfib_map F f bb₁ bb₂ ff₁ β₁ ff₂ β₂ over₁ over₂ cart₁ cart₂.
  Let ζinv : bb₂ --> bb₁
    := lift_unique_sopfib_map F f bb₂ bb₁ ff₂ β₂ ff₁ β₁ over₂ over₁ cart₂ cart₁.

  
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ F e, b ⟧
bb₁, bb₂: E
ff₁: E ⟦ e, bb₁ ⟧
β₁: z_iso b (F bb₁)
ff₂: E ⟦ e, bb₂ ⟧
β₂: z_iso b (F bb₂)
over₁: # F ff₁ = f · β₁
over₂: # F ff₂ = f · β₂
cart₁: is_opcartesian_sopfib F ff₁
cart₂: is_opcartesian_sopfib F ff₂
ζ:= lift_unique_sopfib_map F f bb₁ bb₂ ff₁ β₁ ff₂ β₂
  over₁ over₂ cart₁ cart₂: E ⟦ bb₁, bb₂ ⟧
ζinv:= lift_unique_sopfib_map F f bb₂ bb₁ ff₂ β₂ ff₁ β₁
  over₂ over₁ cart₂ cart₁: E ⟦ bb₂, bb₁ ⟧
ζ · ζinv = identity bb₁

       bb₁ ff₂ β₂ ff₁ β₁ over₂ over₁) = identity bb₁

ff₂: E ⟦ e, bb₂ ⟧
β₂: z_iso b (F bb₂)
over₁: # F ff₁ = f · β₁
over₂: # F ff₂ = f · β₂
cart₁: is_opcartesian_sopfib F ff₁
cart₂: is_opcartesian_sopfib F ff₂
ζ:= lift_unique_sopfib_map F f bb₁ bb₂ ff₁ β₁ ff₂ β₂
  over₁ over₂ cart₁ cart₂: E ⟦ bb₁, bb₂ ⟧
ζinv:= lift_unique_sopfib_map F f bb₂ bb₁ ff₂ β₂ ff₁ β₁
  over₂ over₁ cart₂ cart₁: E ⟦ bb₂, bb₁ ⟧
# F ff₁ = # F ff₁ · identity (F bb₁)

f: B ⟦ F e, b ⟧
bb₁, bb₂: E
ff₁: E ⟦ e, bb₁ ⟧
β₁: z_iso b (F bb₁)
ff₂: E ⟦ e, bb₂ ⟧
β₂: z_iso b (F bb₂)
over₁: # F ff₁ = f · β₁
over₂: # F ff₂ = f · β₂
cart₁: is_opcartesian_sopfib F ff₁
cart₂: is_opcartesian_sopfib F ff₂
ζ:= lift_unique_sopfib_map F f bb₁ bb₂ ff₁ β₁ ff₂ β₂
  over₁ over₂ cart₁ cart₂: E ⟦ bb₁, bb₂ ⟧
ζinv:= lift_unique_sopfib_map F f bb₂ bb₁ ff₂ β₂ ff₁ β₁
  over₂ over₁ cart₂ cart₁: E ⟦ bb₂, bb₁ ⟧
ζ · ζinv = identity bb₁

e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ F e, b ⟧
bb₁, bb₂: E

β₁: z_iso b (F bb₁)
ff₂: E ⟦ e, bb₂ ⟧
β₂: z_iso b (F bb₂)
over₁: # F ff₁ = f · β₁
over₂: # F ff₂ = f · β₂
cart₁: is_opcartesian_sopfib F ff₁
cart₂: is_opcartesian_sopfib F ff₂

  over₁ over₂ cart₁ cart₂: E ⟦ bb₁, bb₂ ⟧
ζinv:= lift_unique_sopfib_map F f bb₂ bb₁ ff₂ β₂ ff₁ β₁
  over₂ over₁ cart₂ cart₁: E ⟦ bb₂, bb₁ ⟧
ζinv · ζ = identity bb₂

x: B ⟦ b, F (pr1 φ₂) ⟧

        apply isaprop_is_z_isomorphism.

  exact Hf₁.

 abstract
      (use invproofirrelevance ;
       intros φ₁ φ₂ ;
       use subtypePath ; [ intro ; apply isapropdirprod ; apply homset_property | ] ;
       refine (!(id_left _) @ _ @ id_left _) ;
       rewrite <- (z_iso_after_z_iso_inv i_iso) ;
       cbn ;
       rewrite !assoc' ;
       rewrite (pr22 φ₁), (pr22 φ₂) ;
       apply idpath).

C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
i: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hi: is_z_isomorphism i
i_iso:= make_z_iso' i Hi: z_iso x₁ x₂
w: C₁
g: C₁ ⟦ x₁, w ⟧
h: C₂ ⟦ F x₂, F w ⟧
p: # F g = # F i · h
# F (inv_from_z_iso i_iso · g) = h
 abstract
        (rewrite functor_comp ;
         rewrite p ;
         rewrite !assoc ;
         rewrite <- functor_comp ;
         etrans ;
           [ apply maponpaths_2 ;
             apply maponpaths ;
             exact (z_iso_after_z_iso_inv i_iso)
           | ] ;
         rewrite functor_id ;
         apply id_left).
    
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂

(λ _ : # F (inv_from_z_iso i_iso · g) = h,
 i · (inv_from_z_iso i_iso · g) = g)
  (iso_is_opcartesian_sopfib_subproof0 C₁ C₂ F x₁ x₂ i
     Hi w g h p)
 abstract
        (cbn ;
         rewrite !assoc ;
         refine (_ @ id_left _) ;
         apply maponpaths_2 ;
         exact (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso i_iso)).
Defined.

Section CompositionOpCartesian.
  Context {C₁ C₂ : category}
          (F : C₁ ⟶ C₂)
          {x₁ x₂ x₃ : C₁}
          {f : x₁ --> x₂}
          (Hf : is_opcartesian_sopfib F f)
          {g : x₂ --> x₃}
          (Hg : is_opcartesian_sopfib F g).

  Section Factorization.
    Context {w : C₁}
            {h₁ : x₁ --> w}
            {h₂ : F x₃ --> F w}
            (p : # F h₁ = # F (f · g) · h₂).

    
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_opcartesian_sopfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_opcartesian_sopfib F g
w: C₁
h₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, w ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F x₃, F w ⟧
p: # F h₁ = # F (f · g) · h₂
C₁ ⟦ x₂, w ⟧

    
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_opcartesian_sopfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_opcartesian_sopfib F g
w: C₁
h₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, w ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F x₃, F w ⟧
p: # F h₁ = # F (f · g) · h₂
C₁ ⟦ x₂, w ⟧

      
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_opcartesian_sopfib F f

p: # F h₁ = # F (f · g) · h₂
# F h₁ = # F f · (# F g · h₂)

      abstract
        (refine (p @ _) ;
         rewrite functor_comp ;
         rewrite !assoc ;
         apply idpath).
    Defined.

h₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, w ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F x₃, F w ⟧
p: # F h₁ = # F (f · g) · h₂
C₁ ⟦ x₂, w ⟧
 exact comp_is_opcartesian_sopfib_factor_help.

· opcartesian_factorization_sopfib F Hg
    (opcartesian_factorization_sopfib F Hf h₁
       (# F g · h₂)
       comp_is_opcartesian_sopfib_factor_help_subproof)
    h₂
    (opcartesian_factorization_sopfib_over F Hf h₁
       (# F g · h₂)
       comp_is_opcartesian_sopfib_factor_help_subproof) =
h₁

w: C₁

h₂: C₂ ⟦ F x₃, F w ⟧
p: # F h₁ = # F (f · g) · h₂
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ φ : C₁ ⟦ x₃, w ⟧, # F φ = h₂ × f · g · φ = h₁
# F h₁ = # F f · (# F g · h₂)

C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_opcartesian_sopfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_opcartesian_sopfib F g
is_opcartesian_sopfib F (f · g)

p: # F h₁ = # F (f · g) · h₂
∃! φ : C₁ ⟦ x₃, w ⟧, # F φ = h₂ × f · g · φ = h₁

  (∑ φ : C₁ ⟦ x₃, w ⟧, # F φ = h₂ × f · g · φ = h₁)

p: # F h₁ = # F (f · g) · h₂
isaprop
  (∑ φ : C₁ ⟦ x₃, w ⟧, # F φ = h₂ × f · g · φ = h₁)
 exact (comp_is_opcartesian_sopfib_factor_unique p).
    
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_opcartesian_sopfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_opcartesian_sopfib F g
w: C₁
h₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, w ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F x₃, F w ⟧
p: # F h₁ = # F (f · g) · h₂
∑ φ : C₁ ⟦ x₃, w ⟧, # F φ = h₂ × f · g · φ = h₁

C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂

 exact (comp_is_opcartesian_sopfib_factor p).
      
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧

g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧

w: C₁

h₂: C₂ ⟦ F x₃, F w ⟧
p: # F h₁ = # F (f · g) · h₂
# F (comp_is_opcartesian_sopfib_factor p) = h₂
 exact (comp_is_opcartesian_sopfib_factor_over p).
      
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_opcartesian_sopfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_opcartesian_sopfib F g
w: C₁
h₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, w ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F x₃, F w ⟧
p: # F h₁ = # F (f · g) · h₂
(λ _ : # F (comp_is_opcartesian_sopfib_factor p) = h₂,
 f · g · comp_is_opcartesian_sopfib_factor p = h₁)
  (comp_is_opcartesian_sopfib_factor_over p)
 exact (comp_is_opcartesian_sopfib_factor_comm p).
  Defined.
End CompositionOpCartesian.
